<Tag slot="tag">

<TagTitle slot="title">

# Pokemon Endpoints

</TagTitle>

<TagDescription slot="description">

Pokémon are the creatures that inhabit the world of the Pokémon games. They can be caught using Pokéballs and trained by battling with other Pokémon. Each Pokémon belongs to a specific species but may take on a variant which makes it differ from other Pokémon of the same species, such as base stats, available abilities and typings. See [Bulbapedia](http://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_(species)) for greater detail.

</TagDescription>

</Tag>

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>GET</b></Pill> /api/v2/ability/ \{#operation-api_v2_ability_list\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

Abilities provide passive effects for Pokémon in battle or in the overworld. Pokémon have multiple possible abilities but can have only one ability at a time. Check out [Bulbapedia](http://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Ability) for greater detail.

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

<CodeSampleTabbedSection>

>

cURL

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent slot="content" id="operation-api_v2_ability_list_code-samples_curl">

<CodeSample>

```curl
curl https://pokeapi.co/api/v2/ability/ \
 -X GET
```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

</CodeSampleTabbedSection>

</OperationCodeSamplesSection>

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

Abilities provide passive effects for Pokémon in battle or in the overworld. Pokémon have multiple possible abilities but can have only one ability at a time. Check out [Bulbapedia](http://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Ability) for greater detail.

</OperationSummarySection>

```json
{
  "effect_changes": [
    {
      "effect_entries": [
        {
          "effect": "ipsum eiusmod",
          "language": {
            "name": "consequat do",
            "url": "reprehenderit ut dolore"
          }
        }
      ],
      "version_group": {
        "name": "occaecat dolor sit",
        "url": "nostrud"
      }
    }
  ],
  "effect_entries": [
    {
      "effect": "aute aliqua aute commodo",
      "language": {
        "name": "irure",
        "url": "dolor"
      },
      "short_effect": "sunt"
    }
  ],
  "flavor_text_entries": [
    {
      "flavor_text": "nisi minim commodo irure minim",
      "language": {
        "name": "do do sint mollit",
        "url": "occaecat"
      },
      "version_group": {
        "name": "fugiat",
        "url": "non nisi proident Lorem"
      }
    }
  ],
  "generation": {
    "name": "nostrud anim",
    "url": "exercitation aliqua sint"
  },
  "id": 87,
  "name": "ut sint",
  "names": [
    {
      "language": {
        "name": "dolor voluptate eu",
        "url": "quis minim non magna quis"
      },
      "name": "et voluptate"
    }
  ],
  "pokemon": [
    {
      "is_hidden": false,
      "pokemon": {
        "name": "gloom",
        "url": "https://pokeapi.co/api/v2/pokemon/44/"
      },
      "slot": "3"
    }
  ]
}
```

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>GET</b></Pill> /api/v2/characteristic/ \{#operation-api_v2_characteristic_list\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_List charecterictics_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Characteristics indicate which stat contains a Pokémon's highest IV. A Pokémon's Characteristic is determined by the remainder of its highest IV divided by 5 (gene_modulo). Check out [Bulbapedia](http://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Characteristic) for greater detail.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>GET</b></Pill> /api/v2/egg-group/ \{#operation-api_v2_egg_group_list\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_List egg groups_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Egg Groups are categories which determine which Pokémon are able to interbreed. Pokémon may belong to either one or two Egg Groups. Check out [Bulbapedia](http://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Egg_Group) for greater detail.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>GET</b></Pill> /api/v2/growth-rate/\{id\}/ \{#operation-api_v2_growth_rate_retrieve\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Get growth rate_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Growth rates are the speed with which Pokémon gain levels through experience. Check out [Bulbapedia](http://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Experience) for greater detail.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

<CodeSampleTabbedSection>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-api_v2_growth_rate_retrieve_code-samples_curl"
  tags={{"codeSample":"curl"}}
>

cURL

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent slot="content" id="operation-api_v2_growth_rate_retrieve_code-samples_curl">

<CodeSample>

```curl
curl https://pokeapi.co/api/v2/growth-rate/{id}/ \
 -X GET
```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

</CodeSampleTabbedSection>

</OperationCodeSamplesSection>

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>GET</b></Pill> /api/v2/pokemon/ \{#operation-api_v2_pokemon_list\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_List pokemon_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Pokémon are the creatures that inhabit the world of the Pokémon games. They can be caught using Pokéballs and trained by battling with other Pokémon. Each Pokémon belongs to a specific species but may take on a variant which makes it differ from other Pokémon of the same species, such as base stats, available abilities and typings. See [Bulbapedia](http://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_(species)) for greater detail.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>GET</b></Pill> /api/v2/pokemon-color/ \{#operation-api_v2_pokemon_color_list\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_List pokemon colors_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Colors used for sorting Pokémon in a Pokédex. The color listed in the Pokédex is usually the color most apparent or covering each Pokémon's body. No orange category exists; Pokémon that are primarily orange are listed as red or brown.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

<CodeSampleTabbedSection>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-api_v2_pokemon_color_list_code-samples_curl"
  tags={{"codeSample":"curl"}}
>

cURL

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent slot="content" id="operation-api_v2_pokemon_color_list_code-samples_curl">

<CodeSample>

```curl
curl https://pokeapi.co/api/v2/pokemon-color/ \
 -X GET
```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

</CodeSampleTabbedSection>

</OperationCodeSamplesSection>

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>GET</b></Pill> /api/v2/pokemon-color/\{id\}/ \{#operation-api_v2_pokemon_color_retrieve\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Get pokemon color_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Colors used for sorting Pokémon in a Pokédex. The color listed in the Pokédex is usually the color most apparent or covering each Pokémon's body. No orange category exists; Pokémon that are primarily orange are listed as red or brown.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>GET</b></Pill> /api/v2/pokemon-form/ \{#operation-api_v2_pokemon_form_list\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_List pokemon forms_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Some Pokémon may appear in one of multiple, visually different forms. These differences are purely cosmetic. For variations within a Pokémon species, which do differ in more than just visuals, the 'Pokémon' entity is used to represent such a variety.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

<CodeSampleTabbedSection>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-api_v2_pokemon_form_list_code-samples_curl"
  tags={{"codeSample":"curl"}}
>

cURL

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent slot="content" id="operation-api_v2_pokemon_form_list_code-samples_curl">

<CodeSample>

```curl
curl https://pokeapi.co/api/v2/pokemon-form/ \
 -X GET
```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

</CodeSampleTabbedSection>

</OperationCodeSamplesSection>

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>GET</b></Pill> /api/v2/pokemon-form/\{id\}/ \{#operation-api_v2_pokemon_form_retrieve\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Get pokemon form_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Some Pokémon may appear in one of multiple, visually different forms. These differences are purely cosmetic. For variations within a Pokémon species, which do differ in more than just visuals, the 'Pokémon' entity is used to represent such a variety.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

<CodeSampleTabbedSection>

  slot="tab"
  id="operation-api_v2_pokemon_form_retrieve_code-samples_curl"
  tags={{"codeSample":"curl"}}
>

</CodeSampleTab>

```curl
curl https://pokeapi.co/api/v2/pokemon-form/{id}/ \
 -X GET
```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

</CodeSampleTabbedSection>

</OperationCodeSamplesSection>

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>GET</b></Pill> /api/v2/pokemon-species/ \{#operation-api_v2_pokemon_species_list\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_List pokemon species_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

A Pokémon Species forms the basis for at least one Pokémon. Attributes of a Pokémon species are shared across all varieties of Pokémon within the species. A good example is Wormadam; Wormadam is the species which can be found in three different varieties, Wormadam-Trash, Wormadam-Sandy and Wormadam-Plant.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

<CodeSampleTabbedSection>

  slot="tab"

>

</CodeSampleTab>

 -X GET
```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

      "pokemon": {
        "name": "bulbasaur",
        "url": "https://pokeapi.co/api/v2/pokemon/1/"
      }
    }
  ]
}
```

</SectionContent>

</ResponseExamplesTabbedSection>

</OperationResponseBodyExamplesSection>

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>GET</b></Pill> /api/v2/pokeathlon-stat/ \{#operation-api_v2_pokeathlon_stat_list\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_List pokeathlon stats_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Pokeathlon Stats are different attributes of a Pokémon's performance in Pokéathlons. In Pokéathlons, competitions happen on different courses; one for each of the different Pokéathlon stats. See [Bulbapedia](http://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Pok%C3%A9athlon) for greater detail.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

<CodeSampleTabbedSection>

  slot="tab"

  tags={{"codeSample":"curl"}}
>

cURL

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent slot="content" id="operation-api_v2_pokeathlon_stat_list_code-samples_curl">

<CodeSample>

```curl
curl https://pokeapi.co/api/v2/pokeathlon-stat/ \
 -X GET
```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

</CodeSampleTabbedSection>

</OperationCodeSamplesSection>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>GET</b></Pill> /api/v2/pokeathlon-stat/\{id\}/ \{#operation-api_v2_pokeathlon_stat_retrieve\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Get pokeathlon stat_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Pokeathlon Stats are different attributes of a Pokémon's performance in Pokéathlons. In Pokéathlons, competitions happen on different courses; one for each of the different Pokéathlon stats. See [Bulbapedia](http://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Pok%C3%A9athlon) for greater detail.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>GET</b></Pill> /api/v2/stat/ \{#operation-api_v2_stat_list\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_List stats_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Stats determine certain aspects of battles. Each Pokémon has a value for each stat which grows as they gain levels and can be altered momentarily by effects in battles.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

  id="operation-api_v2_stat_retrieve_responses_200_application-json"
>

```json
{
  "affecting_moves": {
    "decrease": [
      {
        "change": "5",
        "move": {
          "name": "growl",
          "url": "https://pokeapi.co/api/v2/move/45/"
        }
      }
    ],
    "increase": [
      {
        "change": "-1",
        "move": {
          "name": "swords-dance",
          "url": "https://pokeapi.co/api/v2/move/14/"
        }
      }
    ]
  },
  "affecting_natures": {
    "decrease": [
      {
        "name": "bold",
        "url": "https://pokeapi.co/api/v2/nature/2/"
      }
    ],
    "increase": [
      {
        "name": "lonely",
        "url": "https://pokeapi.co/api/v2/nature/6/"
      }
    ]
  },
  "characteristics": [
    {
      "url": "sunt"
    }
  ],
  "game_index": 56,
  "id": 91,
  "move_damage_class": {
    "name": "nisi minim commodo irure minim",
    "url": "do do sint mollit"
  },
  "name": "occaecat",
  "names": [
    {
      "language": {
        "name": "fugiat",
        "url": "non nisi proident Lorem"
      },
      "name": "nostrud anim"
    }
  ]
}
```

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>GET</b></Pill> /api/v2/type/ \{#operation-api_v2_type_list\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_List types_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Types are properties for Pokémon and their moves. Each type has three properties: which types of Pokémon it is super effective against, which types of Pokémon it is not very effective against, and which types of Pokémon it is completely ineffective against.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

<CodeSampleTabbedSection>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-api_v2_type_list_code-samples_curl"
  tags={{"codeSample":"curl"}}
>

cURL

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent slot="content" id="operation-api_v2_type_list_code-samples_curl">

<CodeSample>

```curl
curl https://pokeapi.co/api/v2/type/ \
 -X GET
```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

</CodeSampleTabbedSection>

</OperationCodeSamplesSection>

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>GET</b></Pill> /api/v2/type/\{id\}/ \{#operation-api_v2_type_retrieve\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Get types_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Types are properties for Pokémon and their moves. Each type has three properties: which types of Pokémon it is super effective against, which types of Pokémon it is not very effective against, and which types of Pokémon it is completely ineffective against.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

<CodeSampleTabbedSection>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-api_v2_type_retrieve_code-samples_curl"
  tags={{"codeSample":"curl"}}
>

cURL

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent slot="content" id="operation-api_v2_type_retrieve_code-samples_curl">

<CodeSample>

```curl
curl https://pokeapi.co/api/v2/type/{id}/ \
 -X GET
```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

</CodeSampleTabbedSection>

</OperationCodeSamplesSection>
